src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:282: // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:283: // asprintf — Render into a heap-allocated buffer, sized to fit the output.
src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:284: //
src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:285: // Unlike sprintf/snprintf, asprintf does not require the caller to pre-size a
src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:286: // buffer. It renders into the 4096-uint8 stack buffer first; if the output fits,
src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:287: // it allocates exactly (len+1) bytes and copies. If the format output exceeds
src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:288: // 4095 bytes, the result is truncated (@cast_unchecked<snprintf>(same) — a known limitation
src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:289: // lifted in v0.7.x when the growable buffer is introduced).
src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:290: //
src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:291: // Returns a heap pointer (as int64) that the caller must free with mem_free().
src/io/bio/fprintf.npk:292: // Writes the string length (without NUL) to *out_len if out_len != 0.

src/math/math.npk:340: // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
src/math/math.npk:342: // math_popcount — Count set bits (population count / Hamming weight).
src/math/math.npk:343: // Uses the classic parallel bit-sum algorithm (no hardware dependency).
src/math/math.npk:344: pub func:math_popcount = int64(int64:v) {
src/math/math.npk:345: // Parallel popcount — each step pairs up groups of bits and sums them
src/math/math.npk:346: // Step 1: sum pairs of bits
src/math/math.npk:347: int64:x = v;
src/math/math.npk:348: x = x - ((x >> 1i64) & 0x5555555555555555i64);
src/math/math.npk:349: // Step 2: sum nibbles
src/math/math.npk:350: x = (x & 0x3333333333333333i64) + ((x >> 2i64) & 0x3333333333333333i64);
src/math/math.npk:351: // Step 3: sum bytes
src/math/math.npk:352: x = (x + (x >> 4i64)) & 0x0F0F0F0F0F0F0F0Fi64;
src/math/math.npk:353: // Step 4: sum all bytes via multiply trick
src/math/math.npk:354: x = (x * 0x0101010101010101i64) >> 56i64;
src/math/math.npk:355: pass x & 0xFFi64;
src/math/math.npk:356: };
src/math/math.npk:358: // math_clz — Count leading zeros in a 64-bit integer.

src/math/math.npk:360: pub func:math_clz = int64(int64:v) {

src/math/math.npk:362: // Binary search for the highest set bit
src/math/math.npk:363: int64:n = 0i64;
src/math/math.npk:364: if ((v & 0xFFFFFFFF00000000i64) == 0i64) { n = n + 32i64; v = v << 32i64; }
src/math/math.npk:365: if ((v & 0xFFFF000000000000i64) == 0i64) { n = n + 16i64; v = v << 16i64; }
src/math/math.npk:367: if ((v & 0xF000000000000000i64) == 0i64) { n = n + 4i64;  v = v << 4i64;  }
src/math/math.npk:371: };

src/syscall/errno.npk:190: // (6-bit tag uint8). The errno value is stored @cast_unchecked<the>(directly) tag.
